Usage: rratrap.py --inffile <.inf file> [options] *.singlepulse

Group single pulse events and rank them based on the sigma behavior.
Plot DM vs time with different colours for different ranks as follows:
Rank 1 (Other)      : Grey
Rank 2 (RFI)        : Red
Rank 3 (ok)         : Cyan
Rank 4 (good)       : dim blue
Rank 5 (very good)  : dark blue
Rank 6 (excellent)  : Magenta

Options:
  --version             show program's version number and exit
  -h, --help            show this help message and exit
  --CLOSE-DM=CLOSE_DM   DM to below which the signalis considered RFI(Default:
                        2
  --use-configfile      If this flag is set - import the config file for
                        selecting groupingparameters.(Default: do not use a
                        config file.)
  --use-DMplan          If this flag is set - Use the ddplan for selecting
                        groupingparameters. Make sure that you have a
                        corresponding config file containingthe DDplan.
                        (Default: do not use ddplan)
  --vary-group-size     If this flag is set - Use the S/N, pulse width and DM
                        to select groupingparameters. Make sure that you have
                        a corresponding config file containingthe DDplan.
                        (Default: do not vary group size)
  --min-group=MIN_GROUP
                        minimum number of events in a group to no be
                        considered noise.(Default: 45)
  --dm-thresh=DM_THRESH
                        DM threshold to use for nearest neighbour. Suggest a
                        value greater  than the DM step size(Default: 0.5
                        pc/cm^3 - will not work if DM step size is greater
                        than 0.5)
  --time-thresh=TIME_THRESH
                        Time threshold to use for nearest neighbour. Suggest a
                        value that  is a few times the max pulse
                        width(Default: 0.1 s)
  --min-sigma=MIN_SIGMA
                        minimum signal-to-noise above which the group is
                        highly consideredto be astrophysical. (Default: 8.0)
  --no-plot             Do not plot the groups in the DM time plot.(Default:
                        Make a plot)
  --plottype=PLOTTYPE   Make a plot using : 'matplotlib' or 'pgplot'.
  --min-rank-to-plot=MIN_RANKTOPLOT
                        Only groups with rank upto this will plotted.(default:
                        plot                        all except rank 1)
  --min-rank-to-write=MIN_RANKTOWRITE
                        Only info of the groups with rank upto this will
                        written.(default: write all except rank 1)
  --inffile=INFFILE     A .inf file. I suggest a .rfifind.inf file.
  -o OUTBASENM          outfile base name. .groups.txt will be added to the
                        given name.
